Tweetr Documentation
Version: 1.0
Last Updated: 15th Oct, 2022
Author: Youness Bahi

  • Get Score

Get started


#Install the development version
    remotes::install_github("younessbahi/tweetr")

An advanced Twitter scraping package written in R that enables the collection of Tweets and other data without using the Twitter's API.

Some of the benefits from using the Tweetr package:

  • Fetch real-time data.
  • Fetch all tweets.
  • No limit of tweets.
  • No initial setup, import or installation is needed.
  • Anonymous usage.
  • No login or authentication is required.
  • No API key is required.
  • All parameters and filters are working and up to date.
  • Complexity-free.

Contact me at DAyounessbahi@gmail.com if you have any questions or suggestions.

get tweets


# From R:
tw <-
    get_tweets(
        query  = '#Bitcoin',
        .since = '2022-10-10',
        .until = '2022-10-14'
        .count = 100
)

# From curl:
curl -X GET "https://twittr-api.herokuapp.com/search?query=%23Bitcoin&.count=100&.since=2022-10-10&.until=2022-10-14&.minLikes=80" -H "accept: */*"

Get tweets data from custom search with get_tweets() function.

Otherwise, if you choose to make a POST call to the following url
https://twittr-api.herokuapp.com/search? you will be limited to 500 tweets only.

QUERY PARAMETERS

Field Required? Type Description
query No String Can be hashtag, keyword, or a user.
.count No Number Default to -1, this will collect all tweets related to your search unless you specify a number of tweets to collect. Depending on the tweets volume, the process might take a while.
.lat No Number Latitude value to provide for geographical search (ex: 33.575692).
Latitude, longitude, and radius are each necessary parameters for geographical search.
.long No Number Longitude value to provide for geographical search (ex: -7.625285).
Latitude, longitude, and radius are each necessary parameters for geographical search.
.radius No String Match Tweets with Tweet-specific location information that are within a sphere-shaped geographic area. (ex: 100km)
Latitude, longitude, and radius are each necessary parameters for geographical search.
.place No String Match Tweets Nearby a city or country.
.since No Date Filter tweets from a specific date.
Allowed date format: YYYY/MM/DD
.until No Date Filter tweets upto a specific date.
Allowed date format: YYYY/MM/DD
.from No String Collect tweets from a user. (ex: @BillGates)
.to No String Collect tweets mentioning or replying to a specific user.
(ex: @BillGates)
.replies No Logical Set to false by default. if it's true then it will fetch tweets replies only.
.minLikes No Number Tweets with at least (n) likes should be filtered.
.minReplies No Number Tweets with at least (n) replies should be filtered.
.minRetweets No Number Tweets with at least (n) retweets should be filtered.
.verified No Logical If true, only tweets from verified accounts will be filtered.
.hasImage No Logical If true, only tweets with images should be filtered.
.hasVideo No Logical If true, Only tweets with videos should be filtered.
.hasMedia No Logical If true, Only tweets with medias should be filtered.
.hasLinks No Logical If true, Only tweets with links should be filtered.
.url No String Get tweets that only contain links to specific domain names (ex: Oscars.org);
Alternatively, you may type in "oscars" to get all tweets with urls that mention the Oscars term.

get trends


# R example:
tw <- get_trends(id = 3534) #id location for Montreal

# curl example
curl -X GET "https://twittr-api.herokuapp.com/trend?woeid=1" -H "accept: */*"

Get trends data from custom search with get_trends() function.

OR, make a POST call to the following url :
https://twittr-api.herokuapp.com/trend?

QUERY PARAMETERS

Field Required? Type Description
woeid No Number Location id, Default to 1 **worldwide**.
Get list of available locations from here

get locations

                
# R example
data('locID', package = 'tweetr')
print(loc)

# curl example
curl -X GET "https://twittr-api.herokuapp.com/trend/location/list" -H "accept: */*"

Locations data is available within the package data.

To get the list of available locations via API, you need to make a POST call to the following url :
https://twittr-api.herokuapp.com/trend/location/list


QUERY PARAMETERS

No parameter is required.

get score


#R example:
get_score('#Bitcoin')

# Here is a curl example
curl -X GET "https://twittr-api.herokuapp.com/score?keyword=%23Bitcoin" -H "accept: */*"

Get topics and influence authors scores based on a search term or a hashtag with get_score() function.

Or, make a POST call to the following url :
https://twittr-api.herokuapp.com/score?

QUERY PARAMETERS

Field Required? Type Description
keyword Yes String Your target search-term or hashtag to get the influence score of similar topics and users.

Errors

The following error codes are specific to the API:

Error Code Meaning
1003 when you pass an incorrect location id.
1005 This error appears when there is no result found for your search.
1010 This error occurs when you pass an empty request.
